  elseif (community matches-any 5) then

  elseif (community matches-any 6) then

  elseif (community matches-any 7) then
    set local-preference 108
  elseif (community matches-any 8) then
    set local-preference 106
  elseif (community matches-any 9) then
    set local-preference 104
  elseif (community matches-any 15) then
    set local-preference 102
  elseif (community matches-any 16) then
    set local-preference 90
  elseif (community matches-any 17) then
    set local-preference 88
  elseif (community matches-any 18) then
    set local-preference 80

    set local-preference 78
  elseif (community matches-any 20) then
    set local-preference 70
  elseif (community matches-any 21) then
    set local-preference 68
  endif

end-policy

route-policy TRAFICO_CONTROL_ZONA
  if (community matches-any 100) then
    set local-preference 110
  elseif (community matches-any 101) then
    set local-preference 108
  elseif (community matches-any 102) then
    set local-preference 106
  elseif (community matches-any 103) then
    set local-preference 104
  elseif (community matches-any 104) then
    set local-preference 102
  elseif not (community matches-any 105) then
    pass
  endif
end-policy
